Additionally, electrostatic interactions play a significant role, as the electron-rich regions of the calixarene and pyrrole can stabilize the negative charge of the anion. In some cases, anion–π interactions may also contribute, where the anion interacts with the π-system of the aromatic rings in the calixarene or the pyrrole. The overall binding affinity and selectivity are determined by the spatial arrangement of the pyrrole groups, the size and shape of the calixarene cavity, and the nature of the anion.
